SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[NameEn], [t].[NameAr], COALESCE([t].[DescriptionEn], [t].[Description]), [t].[DescriptionAr], [t].[ImageUrl], [t].[Price], [t].[StockQuantity], [t].[CategoryId], [c].[NameEn], [c].[NameAr], [t].[Sku], CASE
    WHEN (
        SELECT COUNT(*)
        FROM [ProductReviews] AS [p0]
        WHERE [t].[Id] = [p0].[ProductId]) > 0 THEN (
        SELECT AVG(CAST([p1].[Rating] AS float))
        FROM [ProductReviews] AS [p1]
        WHERE [t].[Id] = [p1].[ProductId])
    ELSE NULL
END, (
    SELECT COUNT(*)
    FROM [ProductReviews] AS [p2]
    WHERE [t].[Id] = [p2].[ProductId])
FROM (
    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[Description], [p].[DescriptionAr], [p].[DescriptionEn], [p].[ImageUrl], [p].[NameAr], [p].[NameEn], [p].[Price], [p].[Sku], [p].[StockQuantity]
    FROM [Products] AS [p]
    ORDER BY [p].[NameEn]
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]

ORDER BY [t].[NameEn]
